<script>
    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 8; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(8);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

    $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView")

    function LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobDataView() {
        if ($("#dvGridSettings__EmployeeJobDataView").html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridSettings',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeeJobDataView', GridHeight: '800', settings: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSettings__EmployeeJobDataView').html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("Settings__EmployeeJobDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    function LoadSearchSettingsOnDemand(dataViewKey) {
        if ($("#dvGridSearchSettings__" + dataViewKey).html().length &gt; 100) return;
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GridFilter',
            cache: false,
            async: false,
            data: { dataViewName: dataViewKey, GridHeight: '800', gridFilter: null },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#dvGridSearchSettings__' + dataViewKey).html(result);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__" + dataViewKey + ": " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("SearchSettings__EmployeeJobDataView: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    }

    $('#GridSettingsWnd__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobDataView();
        $("#settingsWindow__EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoWindow").center().open();

        //refreshing source grid data
        var gridSource = $("#gridSettings__EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        gridSource.dataSource.read();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/GetOtherGridSettingsOnLoad',
            cache: false,
            data: { dataViewName: 'EmployeeJobDataView' },
            success: function (result) {
                // debugger;
                if (result != null) {
                    // debugger;
                    var ddSortBy = $('#SortBy__EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortBy.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem.Text === result.SortBy;
                    });

                    var ddSortDir = $('#SortDir__EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");

                    ddSortDir.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.SortDir;
                    });

                    var ddPageSize = $('#PageSize__EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddPageSize.select(function (dataItem) {
                        return dataItem === result.PageSize;
                    });
                }
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    $('#ClearGridSettingsWnd__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function () {
        LoadSettingsOnDemand__EmployeeJobDataView();
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/GridConfig/RestoreToDefault',
            cache: false,
            data: {
                gridName: 'EmployeeJobDataView', GridHeight: '800', AutoAdjustHeight:
                          $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeJobDataView').val(),
                verticallyScrollable: 'True',
                selectedRecords: $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid").table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected"),
                isEditable: false
            },
            success: function (result) {
                $('#divEmployeeJobDataView').html(result);
                InitializeGrid___EmployeeJobDataView(false);
                var function_name = 'EmployeeJobDataView__Restore';
                if (typeof (window[function_name]) === "function") {
                    window[function_name]();
                }

                var hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeJobDataView').val();
                if (hdnAutoAdjustHeightVal == "true") {
                    RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeeJobDataView");
                }
                HideGridFooter("EmployeeJobDataView", true);
            },
            error: function (xhr, ajaxOptions, thrownError) {
                alert("ClearGridSettings: " + xhr.status + " " + thrownError + " " + ajaxOptions);
            }
        });
    });

    function MaintainGridState(grid) {
        MaintainGridStateHandler(grid, grid.element[0].id, '/QAAutom/GridConfig/SaveGridState');
    }

    function InitializeGrid___EmployeeJobDataView(fromPageLoad) {
        var autoLoad = 'True' == 'True';
        //debugger;
        if ((fromPageLoad == true) || (!autoLoad)) {
            setTimeout(function () {
                GridGotoPage("EmployeeJobDataView", "1");
            }, 300)
        }
    }

    function PersistGridSelectionOnPageChange(grid) {
        PersistGridSelectionOnPageChangeHandler(grid, this.element[0].id)
    }

    function grid_columnResize__EmployeeJobDataView(e) {
        e.preventDefault = true;
        var grid = e.sender;
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function grid_columnReorder__EmployeeJobDataView(e) {
        var grid = e.sender;
        e.preventDefault = true;
        grid.reorderColumn(e.newIndex, grid.columns[e.oldIndex]);
        MaintainGridState(grid);
    }

    function collapseGroupRows(grid) {
        grid.collapseGroup(grid.tbody.find("&gt;tr.k-grouping-row"));
        $('tr[role*="row"]').hide();
    }

    function PageLoad__EmployeeJobDataView() {
        var gridName = 'EmployeeJobDataView';
        var grid = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        //if its not gridsettings or gridsearchsettings
        if (gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsettings") == -1 || gridName.toLowerCase().indexOf("gridsearchsettings") == -1) {
            //
                InitializeGrid___EmployeeJobDataView(true);
        }
        var hdnAutoAdjustHeight = $('#hdnAutoAdjustHeight_EmployeeJobDataView');

        if (parseBool("True")) {
            RegisterGridForAutoHeight("#" + "EmployeeJobDataView");
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('true');
        }
        else {
            hdnAutoAdjustHeight.val('false');
        }

        var hdnScrollable = $('#hdnScrollable_EmployeeJobDataView');
        hdnScrollable.val('true');
    }
    $(document).ready(function () { PageLoad__EmployeeJobDataView(); });

    function grid_checkbox_onclick(fldName, gridName, theCheckBox) {
        var checked = theCheckBox.checked;
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theCheckBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            eval("dataItem." + fldName + " = checked");
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theCheckBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theCheckBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    function grid_textbox_onchange(fldName, gridName, theTextBox) {
        var gridData = $("#" + gridName).data("kendoGrid");
        var dataItem = gridData.dataItem($(theTextBox).closest('tr'));
        if (typeof dataItem != "undefined" &amp;&amp; dataItem != null) {
            dataItem.dirty = true;
            if ($(theTextBox).closest('td').html().indexOf("k-dirty") &lt; 0)
            { $(theTextBox).closest('td').prepend('&lt;span class="k-dirty"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;'); }
        }
    }

    $('#UnselectAll__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ClearGridSelection();
    });

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {

    $("#btnMassUpdateEmployeeJobs__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = GetGridSelectedId("EmployeeJobDataView");

        if (!$("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) return;

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowMassUpdateEmployeeJobs")
                         .SetContent({ type: "POST", url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassUpdateEmployeeJobs" })
                         .SetIsModal(true)
                         .SetWidth(650)
                         .SetHeight("70%")
                         .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
                         .SetonActivate(function () { RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobsMassUpdate", null); })
                         .SetTitle("Mass Update Employee Jobs");

        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);

    });

    function IsTxnEncumberAllowed() {
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IsTxnEncumberDateAllowed',
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
            },
            success: function (response) {
                //debugger;
                if (response.Success === true) {
                    $("#hdnIsEncumberDateAllowed").val('True');
                }
                else {
                    $("#hdnIsEncumberDateAllowed").val('Flase');
                }
            }
        });
    }
    $('#btnMassIncrementSalaryScheduleGrade__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        MassIncrementSalarySchedule(false);
    });

    $('#btnMassIncrementSalaryScheduleStep__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        MassIncrementSalarySchedule(true);
    });

    function MassIncrementSalarySchedule(isStepUp) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");

        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (typeof selectedRowIds == "undefined" || selectedRowIds == null || selectedRowIds.length == 0) {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            return;
        }
        var heading = isStepUp ? "Increment Salary Schedule Step" : "Increment Salary Schedule Grade";
        var message = isStepUp ? "Are you sure you want to Increment Salary Schedule Step the selected job(s)?" : "Are you sure you want to Increment Salary Schedule Grade the selected job(s)?";
        PerformIncrementSalarySchedule(isStepUp, selectedRowIds, heading, message);
    }

    function PerformIncrementSalarySchedule(isStepUp, selectedRowIds, heading, message) {
        if (isStepUp) {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowIncrementSalarySchedule")
            .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IncrementSalaryScheduleStepPopup?" + "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds + "&amp;isStepUp=" + isStepUp })
        .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
        .SetTitle(heading)
        .SetWidth(600)
        .SetHeight("25%")
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobDataView", null);

        }
        else {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowIncrementSalarySchedule")
            .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IncrementSalaryScheduleGradePopup?" + "selectedRecords=" + selectedRowIds + "&amp;isStepUp=" + isStepUp })
        .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
        .SetTitle(heading)
        .SetWidth(600)
        .SetHeight("25%")
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobDataView", null);
        }

    }

    function EditEmployeeJob(EmployeeId, CycleId, JobSequence) {

        var id = EmployeeId + '~' + CycleId + '~' + JobSequence;
        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
        EditEmployeeJobFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection);
    }

    function EditEmployeeJobFinsWindow(id, aptaDataViewSelection) {
        var data;

        data = { Id: id, aptaDataViewSelection: aptaDataViewSelection, origin: 2 };
        options = { url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob", data: data, type: "POST" };

    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowEmployeeJob")
      .SetIsModal(true)
      .SetContent(options)
      .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
      .SetTitle('Edit Employee Job')
      .SetWidth('1220')
      .SetHeight('90%')
    finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobsDataView", null);
    }

    function OnPageLoad() {
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, null, "EmployeeJobDataView");
        $("#btnAdd__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowEmployeeJob")
               .SetIsModal(true)
               .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/CreateJob" + "?employeeID=0&amp;origin=2" })
           .SetTitle('Add Employee Job')
           .SetWidth('1220')
           .SetHeight('90%')
           .SetUnRegisterShortCutKeysOnClose(true)
            finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeJobsDataView", null);
        });

        $("#btnEdit__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            var grid = $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView");
            if (grid.ValidateDataViewGridSelection(true, "Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.")) {
                var aptaDataViewSelection = grid.GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                EditEmployeeJobFinsWindow("", aptaDataViewSelection);
            }
        });

        $("#btnDelete__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
            var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0)
                ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm Delete", "Are you sure you want to delete the selected records?", function () { DeleteEmployeeJob(); });
            else {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            }
        });

        var submitForAllNo = false;
        var submitForAllYes = false;
        $('#btnApproveJob__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            ShowAjaxMessage("", "");

            submitForAllNo = false;
            submitForAllYes = false;

            var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
            var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

            if (NoItemsSelected(selectedRowIds)) {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
                return;
            }

            if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0) {
                ShowYesNoDialog("Approve Job", "Are you sure you want to approve the selected job(s)?", function () { ApproveJobDialogue(); });
            }
            else {
                ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
            }

        });

    }
    var submitForAllNo = false;
    var submitForAllYes = false;

    function RefreshOnApproveJobs(jobID, inProcessRegisterWarning, moveNext, overbudget) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var key = '';
        $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/ApproveJob',
                     { jobID: jobID, moveNext: moveNext, massOpertaionId: massOperationId, inProcessRegisterWarning: inProcessRegisterWarning, overbudget: overbudget, origin: "2", aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView") },
                key, function (result) {

                    if (result.Success == 1) {
                        RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, false);

                    }

                    else if (result.Success == 3) {
                        if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, true);
                        }
                        else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, true, false);
                        }
                        else {

                            ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Approve Job", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, true); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, true, false); submitForAllNo = e; });
                        }
                    }

                    else if (result.Success == 5) {

                        if (submitForAllYes === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, false, true);
                        }
                        else if (submitForAllNo === true) {
                            RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, true, true);
                        }
                        else {
                            ShowYesNoDialogWithCheckBox("Approve Job", result.Message, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, false, true); submitForAllYes = e; }, function (e) { RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, false, true, true); submitForAllNo = e; });

                        }
                    }
                    else if (result.Success == 4) {
                        //4 indicates process end,
                        submitForAllNo = false;
                        submitForAllYes = false;
                        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                        ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                        ShowMassActionResultsPopup('popupwindowMassActionResults');

                    }
                    else {
                        RefreshOnApproveJobs(result.JobId, true, false, true);
                    }
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults", false);
    }

    function ApproveJobDialogue() {
        // check if the config values are present, if yes then show the dialogue.
        var showTransactionDatesPopup = $("#hdnIsEncumberDateAllowed").val();

        var aptaDV = $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView");
        var data = { aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView"), origin: "2" };
        //var encumberWages = false;
        aptaDV.MakeAjaxCall({
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DoesIncludeEncumberJobWages",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                alert(error);
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (showTransactionDatesPopup === "True" &amp;&amp; result.Success == 1) {
                    ShowApproveJobDatePopup("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/ApproveJobEnterDate");
                }
                else {
                    var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnApproveJobs(-1, true, false, false); });
                    finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function ShowApproveJobDatePopup(contentURL) {

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("EmployeeJobsManageApproveJobDatePopup")
            .SetContent({ url: contentURL })
            .SetIsModal(true).SetonClose(UnRegisterActiveScreen())
            .SetTitle('Approve Job(s)')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
        RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, "EmployeeApproveJobDate", null);

    }

    function RefreshOnCloseEmployeeJob(selectedRowIds) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        var key = '';
        $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CloseEmployeeJob',
                     { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, origin: "2", aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView") },
                key, function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    $("#btnCloseJob__EmployeeJobDataView").click(function (e) {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0)
            ShowYesNoDialog("Close Job", "Are you sure you want to close the selected job(s)?", function () {
                var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");
                var showTransactionDatesPopup = $("#hdnIsEncumberDateAllowed").val();

                var aptaDV = $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView");
                var data = { aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView"), origin: "2" };
                var encumberWages = false;
                aptaDV.MakeAjaxCall({
                    url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DoesIncludeEncumberJob",
                    data: data,
                    dataType: "json",
                    error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                        alert(error);
                    },
                    success: function (result) {
                        if (showTransactionDatesPopup === "True" &amp;&amp; result.Success == 1) {
                            ShowCloseJobDatePopup("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/CloseJobEnterDate");
                        }
                        else {
                            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnCloseEmployeeJob(selectedRowIds); });
                            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
                        }
                    }
                });

            });
        else {
            ShowOkDialog("Selection", "Please select one or more records for this operation.", null);
        }
    });

    function RefreshOnDeleteEmployeeJob(selectedRowIds) {
        var massOperationId = GetMassActionId();

        $("#divEmployeeJobDataView").data("AptaDataView").ExecuteMassOperation('/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DeleteEmployeeJob',
                    { massOpertaionId: massOperationId, selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, origin: "2", aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView") },
                '', function (result) {
                    var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
                    ClearGridSelectionAndReload(grid, "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }, "popupwindowMassActionResults");
    }

    function DeleteEmployeeJob() {

        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateMassActionWindowObject({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassActionResults" }).SetonRefresh(function () { RefreshOnDeleteEmployeeJob(selectedRowIds); });
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(false);
    };

    function ApproveJobsWithWarning(inProcessRegisterWarning) {

        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        // debugger;
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/ApproveJob',
            cache: false,
            data: { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, inProcessRegisterWarning: inProcessRegisterWarning, origin: "2" },
            success: function (result) {

                //refresh grid
                grid.dataSource.read();
                if (result == "") {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Job approved successfully.", "success");

                    //removing selection from the attributes.
                    grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected", "");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                }

            }
        });
    }

    function VacatePosition() {
        var grid = $("#EmployeeJobDataView").data("kendoGrid");
        var selectedRowIds = grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected");

        var data = { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, origin: "2", aptaDataViewSelection: AptaFundDataView.AptaDataView.GetAptaDataViewSelectionByName("EmployeeJobDataView") };
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/VacatePositionEmployeeJob',
            type: "POST",
            cache: false,
            data: data,
            success: function (result) {
                grid.dataSource.read();
                if (result == "") {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Job vacated successfully.", "success");

                    //removing selection from the attributes.
                    grid.table.attr("data-AptaFund-KendoGrid-selected", "");
                    grid.thead.find("tr .selectAll__EmployeeJobDataView").attr("checked", false);
                    SetGridSelectedRecords("EmployeeJobDataView", "/QAAutom/GridConfig/SetGridSelectedRecords");
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result, "error");
                }
            }
        });
    };

    function MassApproveJobs() {
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/QAAutom/Employee/IsActiveJobInMassApproveSelectedEmployees",
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (returnData) {
                //debugger;
                if (!returnData) {
                    //redirect to Mass Job approve grid
                    window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassApproveJob?fromSearch=False";
                }
                else {
                    ShowYesNoDialog("Mass Approve", "One or more of the selected jobs may be part of a Payroll Register that is currently being processed. Any changes that have been made to the job(s) will not affect this register. To have the changes apply to the in-process register, the job(s) will have to be removed from the register before running this process. Do you want to continue with the Mass Job Approval?", function () {
                        window.location.href = "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/MassApproveJob?fromSearch=False";
                    });
                }

            },
            error: function (e) {
                //debugger;
            }
        });

    }

    $('#btnMassApproveJob__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function () {

        MassApproveJobs();
    });

    $('#btnRolloverEmployeeJobs__EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        OpenRolloverEmployeeJobWnd();
    });

    function OpenRolloverEmployeeJobWnd() {

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/IsNextCycleAvailable',
            cache: false,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if (!result) {
                    ShowOkDialog("Notice", "No next cycle available for rollover job process.", null);
                    return;
                }
                var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowRolloverEmployeeJob")
                            .SetContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/RolloverEmployeeJob" }).SetIsModal(true).SetHeight(430).SetWidth(640)
                .SetTitle('Rollover Employee Jobs').SetonDeactivate(function () { UnRegisterActiveScreen(); });
                finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
            }
        });

    }
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }

<script>

    var isCalculationInProgress =false;

    function UpdateAllFields(IsDateChange, IsSalaryDataChange)
    {

        $("#TotalSalary").removeAttr("data-val-required");
        $("#StartDate").removeAttr("data-val-required");
        $("#JobType").removeAttr("data-val-required");
        $("#MasterPositionId").removeAttr("data-val-required");
        $("#FTE").removeAttr("data-val-required");

        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "EmployeeJobDetail_Error");

        var startDate = $("#StartDate").data("FINSDatePicker").GetFormatedValue();
        var endDate =  $("#EndDate").data("FINSDatePicker").GetFormatedValue();
        var fte = $("#FTE").val();
        var hourlyRate = $("#HourlyRate").data('kendoNumericTextBox').value();
        var hoursPerDay = $("#HoursPerDay").val();
        var masterPositionId = $("#MasterPositionId").val();
        var positionId = $("#EJPositionId").val();
        var ssStepId = $("#SSStepId").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
        var jobType = $('#JobType').val();
        var controlled = $("#Controlled").val();
        var calendarId = $("#CalendarId").val();
        var cycleSalary =  $("#Salary").val();
        var updateSalary = true;
        var totalContractDays= $("#TotalContractDays").val();
        var ContractDays = $("#ContractDays").val();
        var jobSequence =$('#JobSequence').val();
        var cycleId = $('#CycleId').val();
        var isMultiYear= $("#IsMultiYear").data("FINSUICheckbox").Value;
        var totalSalary= $("#TotalSalary").val();

        if (jobType == '' || (jobType == 'Salary' &amp;&amp; ssStepId == ""))
        {
            updateSalary = false;
        }

        var data = {
            startDate : startDate,
            endDate: endDate,
            fte : fte,
            hourlyRate : hourlyRate,
            hoursPerDay : hoursPerDay,
            masterPositionId: masterPositionId,
            positionId : positionId,
            SSStepId:ssStepId,
            JobType :jobType,
            controlled : controlled,
            calendarId: calendarId,
            cycleSalary : cycleSalary,
            updateSalary : updateSalary,
            totalContractDays : totalContractDays,
            jobSequence:jobSequence,
            IsDateChange:IsDateChange,
            cycleId: cycleId,
            IsMultiYear: isMultiYear,
            totalSalary : totalSalary,
            IsSalaryDataChange:IsSalaryDataChange,
            CycleContractDays : ContractDays

        };

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/CalculateSalaryFields',
            cache: false,
            data: data,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if(result.Success)
                    SetValues(false,result.dc, data);
            }
        });

    }

    function SetValues(masterPositionChanged,result, data,stepChange)
    {

        if(masterPositionChanged)
        {
            $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue(result.AccountCode);
            $("#hdnAccountStagingId_MultipleAccountCodeGrid_AcEmployeeJobDetails").val(result.StagingId);
            $("#AccountStagingId").val(result.StagingId);
            if(result.AccountCode !='Multiple')
            {
                SetLabelDescriptionAccountCode('lblAccountDesc_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox', result.AccountCode);
            }
            //JobType
            if (result.MasterPositionType != null &amp;&amp; result.MasterPositionType != '') {
                $("#JobType").data("FINSComboBox").SetValue(result.MasterPositionType);
            }
            $("#Designation").data("FINSComboBox").DataParameters.MasterPositionId = result.MasterPositionId;
            $("#Designation").data("kendoComboBox").dataSource.read();
            //Start Date
            if (result.StartDate != null &amp;&amp; result.StartDate != '')
                $("#StartDate").data("FINSDatePicker").SetValue(result.StartDate);
            //Endate
            if (result.EndDate != null &amp;&amp; result.EndDate != '')
                $("#EndDate").data("FINSDatePicker").SetValue(result.EndDate);
            //FTE
            if (result.FTE != null)
                $("#FTE").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetValue(result.FTE);
            else
                $("#FTE").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetValue(0);
            //Hourly Rate
            if (result.HourlyRate != null &amp;&amp; result.HourlyRate != '')
                $("#HourlyRate").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetValue(result.HourlyRate);
            //Hours PEr day
            if (result.HoursPerDay != null &amp;&amp; result.HoursPerDay != '')
                $("#HoursPerDay").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetValue(result.HoursPerDay);
            //Work Days
            if (result.ContractDays != null &amp;&amp; result.ContractDays != '')
                $("#TotalContractDays").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetValue(result.ContractDays);
            //Calendarid
            if (result.CalendarId != null &amp;&amp; result.CalendarId != '')
                $("#CalendarId").val(result.CalendarId);
            //supplemental
            if (result.Supplemental != null &amp;&amp; result.Supplemental != '')
                $("#Supplemental").val(result.Supplemental);
            //controlled
            if (result.Controlled != null &amp;&amp; result.Controlled != '')
                $("#Controlled").val(result.Controlled);
            if (result.SSName != null) {
                $("#SSName").data('FINSComboBox').SetValue(result.SSName);
                $("#TotalSalary").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetReadOnly(true);
            }
            $("#TotalSalary").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue(result.Salary);

            var p= { SSStepId: result.SSName, JobType : result.MasterPositionType , TotalSalary : result.Salary, HourlyRate : result.HourlyRate,
                UpdateContractDays: false, TotalContractDays: result.TotalContractDays, IsMultiYear : false };
            EnableDisableSetFields(p);

        }
        else
        {
            var category = $("#JobCategory").data("FINSComboBox");
            if(category!=null &amp;&amp; category != typeof(undefined))
            {
                if (data.JobTypePayroll == "N~true" &amp;&amp; data.JobTypePayroll  != null &amp;&amp; data.JobTypePayroll == "Hourly Payment Plan") {
                    $("#JobCategory").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(true);
                }
                else {
                    if($("#ReadOnly").val()!=="True")
                        $("#JobCategory").data("FINSComboBox").SetReadOnly(false);
                }
            }

            var p= { SSStepId: data.SSStepId, JobType : data.JobType , TotalSalary : result.TotalSalary, HourlyRate : result.HourlyRate,
                UpdateContractDays: data.IsDateChange, TotalContractDays: result.TotalContractDays, IsMultiYear : result.IsMultiYear,
                Salary : result.Salary,ContractDays : result.ContractDays
            };
            EnableDisableSetFields(p);

        }

    }

    function EnableDisableSetFields(data){
        $("#HourlyRate").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetReadOnly(false);

        var hasStepId=data.SSStepId!='' &amp;&amp; data.SSStepId != null &amp;&amp; data.SSStepId != typeof(undefined);
        if(hasStepId)
        {
            $("#TotalSalary").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetReadOnly(true);
            $("#Salary").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetReadOnly(true);
        }
        else
        {
            $("#TotalSalary").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetReadOnly(false);
        }

        if(data.JobType == "Salary")
        {
            $("#HourlyRate").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetValue('');
            $("#HourlyRate").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetReadOnly(true);
            $("label[for='TotalSalary']").addClass("RequiredLabel");
            if(hasStepId)
            {
                $("#TotalSalary").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue(data.TotalSalary);
            }
            if($("#TotalSalary").data("FINSUINumberInput").Value != 0)
            {
                // user manullay input salary when job type is salary
                data.TotalSalary =$("#TotalSalary").data("FINSUINumberInput").Value;
            }
        }
        else
        {
            if(hasStepId)
            {
                $("#HourlyRate").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetReadOnly(true);
                $("#HourlyRate").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetValue(data.HourlyRate);
            }
            $("#TotalSalary").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue(data.TotalSalary);
            if (data.JobType == "Hourly") {
                $("#TotalSalary").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetReadOnly(true);
                $("label[for='TotalSalary']").removeClass("RequiredLabel");
            }
            else if (data.JobType == "Daily") {
                $("#TotalSalary").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetReadOnly(true);
                $("label[for='TotalSalary']").removeClass("RequiredLabel");
            }
        }

        if(data.IsMultiYear){
            $("#multiyearsection").show();
            $("#Salary").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue(data.Salary);
            $("#IsMultiYear").data("FINSUICheckbox").Checked(true);
            $("#IsMultiYear").data("FINSUICheckbox").SetReadOnly(true);
            $("#ContractDays").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue(data.ContractDays);

        }
        else{
            $("#multiyearsection").hide();
            $("#Salary").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue(data.TotalSalary);
        }

        if(data.UpdateContractDays)
        {
            $("#TotalContractDays").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetValue(data.TotalContractDays);
        }

        if('0' &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; '' != "N" &amp;&amp; '' != "C" )
        {
            $("#HourlyRate").data("FINSUINumberInput").SetReadOnly(true);
            $("#TotalSalary").data('FINSUINumberInput').SetReadOnly(true);
        }

        var a = $('#Salary').val() - Number('');
        if (!a) { a = null}
        $('#TotalAmnt').val(a);
        isCalculationInProgress=false;
    }

    function OnMasterPositionChange()
    {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "");
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "EmployeeJobDetail_Error");

        var masterPositionId = $("#MasterPositionId").val();
        if(masterPositionId ==null || masterPositionId =='' || masterPositionId == typeof(undefined))
        {
            return;
        }

        var data = {
            masterPositionId: masterPositionId
        };
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/GetDataByPositionId',
            cache: false,
            data: data,
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                if(result.Success)
                    SetValues(true,result.dc);
            }
        });
    }

    function OnDateChange()
    {
        if(isCalculationInProgress==false)
        {
            isCalculationInProgress = true;
            UpdateAllFields(true, true);
        }
    }

    function OnRateAndDaysChange()
    {
        if(isCalculationInProgress==false)
        {
            isCalculationInProgress = true;
            UpdateAllFields(false, true);
        }
    }

    function GradeNameComboChange() {
        $("#SSStepId").data("FINSComboBox").DataParameters.SSName = $("#SSName").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
        $("#SSStepId").data("FINSComboBox").DataParameters.GradeName = $("#GradeName").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
    }
</script>

<script>
    function onRefreshAccountsPopup_AcEmployeeJobDetails(e) {
        e.sender.title('Account Code Allocation');
        e.sender.center();

        setFocusEventForKendoWindow('popupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_' + 'AcEmployeeJobDetails');
    }

    function onActivateAccountsPopup_AcEmployeeJobDetails() {
        if ($("#tbAccountCodeEdit_" + 'AcEmployeeJobDetails' + "acMultipleAccountCode").val() == '') {
            $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_" + 'AcEmployeeJobDetails' + "acMultipleAccountCode").removeAttr("disabled");
        }
    }

    function onCloseRefreshAccountCode_AcEmployeeJobDetails(e) {
        $("pupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_AcEmployeeJobDetails").html('');
        var stagingId = $("#AccountStagingId").val()
        var data = { stagingId: stagingId };

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/GetAccountCode",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    if (result.AccountCode) {
                        $.ajax({
                            cache: false,
                            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/AcAccountTextBox",
                            data: { AccountCode: result.AccountCode, AccountType: 'Expenditure', EnableAccountMask: 'True', Key: 'AcEmployeeJobDetails' + 'acTextBox', AccountCodeWidthEm: "28", AllocationSequence: '0', AcAccountTextBoxOnChangeFunction: '' },
                            dataType: "html",
                            success: function (resp) {
                                $("#AccountCodeBox_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").html(resp);
                                if ('' !== '') {
                                    ;
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                    //debugger;
                    $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").val(result.AccountCode);
                    if (result.AccountCode == "Multiple")
                        $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").select();
                }
            }
        });
    }
</script>

<div class="editor-field">
    <div style="float:left">
    <script>
        function btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox(e) {
            var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowAccountCodeAssistant_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox")
                .SetIsModal(true)
                .SetTitle("Account Code Assistant")
                .SetonActivate(function () { AccountCodeLookUpActivated_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox(); })
                .SetonDeactivate(function () { ReturnFromAccountCodeLookup_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox(); });

            finsWindow.CreateWindow(false).SetHTMLContent('&lt;div id="divACL_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox" &gt;&lt;/div&gt;');
            onAccountCodeLookupWindowOpen_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox();
            finsWindow.OpenWindow();
            e.preventDefault();
        }

        $(function () {
            $("#btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").click(btnOpenAccountCodeAssistant_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox);
        });

        function onAccountCodeLookupWindowOpen_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox(e) {
            var accountType = $("#hdnAccountTypeAcAccountTextBox_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").val();
            //If an account type is selected in account code assistant popup, use that account type.
            if (!$("#tbAccountCodeEdit_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").val() &amp;&amp; $("#ACLAccountType_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox") &amp;&amp; $("#ACLAccountType_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
                accountType = $("#ACLAccountType_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
            }
            var data = {
                AccountType: accountType,
                Key: "AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox",
                AccountCode: $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").val()
            };

            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                async: false,
                url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/AccountCodeLookup",
                data: data,
                success: function (result) {
                    $("#divACL_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").html(result);
                },
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    console.log(textStatus, errorThrown);
                }
            });
        }

        function AccountCodeLookUpActivated_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox(e) {
            SelectedElementValues_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox("tbAccountCodeEdit_" + 'AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox');
        }

        function ReturnFromAccountCodeLookup_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox() {
            if (bOk) {
                bOk = false;
                var accountType
                var AccountId = $('#AccountId_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox').data("kendoComboBox").value();

                if ($("#ACLAccountType_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox") &amp;&amp; $("#ACLAccountType_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value) {
                    accountType = $("#ACLAccountType_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").data("FINSComboBox").Value;
                }
                else {
                    accountType = 'Expenditure';
                }
                $.ajax({
                    cache: false,
                    url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/AcAccountTextBox",
                    data: {
                        AccountCode: AccountId,
                        AccountType: accountType,
                        AccountCodeWidthEm: '28',
                        EnableAccountMask: 'True',
                        Key: 'AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox',
                        AcAccountTextBoxOnChangeFunction: '',
                        HtmlAttributeName: ''
                    },
                    dataType: "html",
                    success: function (resp) {
                        $("#AccountCodeBox_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").html(resp);
                        SetLabelDescriptionAccountCode('lblAccountDesc_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox', AccountId);
                        if ('' !== '') {
                            ;
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }
    </script>

<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var combobox = $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox").data("kendoComboBox");

        combobox.bind("change", function () {
            OnAcAccountTextBoxChangeEvent('AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox', "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/GetAccountDescriptionByCode");
            if ('' != '')
                ;
        });

        SetDescription('AcEmployeeJobDetailsacTextBox');

        function SetDescription(modelKey) {
            var accountCodeValue = $("#tbAccountCodeEdit_" + modelKey).data("kendoComboBox").value();

            if (modelKey.search('acMultipleAccountCode') &lt; 0 || modelKey.search('acMultipleAccountCodeEdit') &gt;= 0) {
                GetDescription(modelKey, "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/GetAccountDescriptionByCode");
            }
        };
    });

    function SetLabelDescriptionAccountCode(labelName, accountCode, width) {
        SetLabelDescriptionForAccountCode(labelName, accountCode, width, "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/GetAccountDescriptionByCode");
    }
</script>

<script>
    function AcMultipleAllocation_GetTotalAmount(unitsFN, unitPriceFN, amountFN, validate, precision) {
        var totalAmount = 0.0;

        if (amountFN != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; amountFN != '') {
            var amount = $("#" + amountFN).val();
            if (typeof amount != 'undefined') {
                if (validate &amp;&amp; (amount == '' || amount == '')) {
                    return null;
                }
                totalAmount = Number(amount);
            }
        }
        else {
            var orderQty = $("#" + unitsFN).val();
            var prUnitPrice = $("#" + unitPriceFN).val();
            if (typeof orderQty != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; (typeof prUnitPrice != 'undefined')) {
                if (validate &amp;&amp; (orderQty == '' || prUnitPrice == '' || orderQty == null || prUnitPrice == null)) {
                    return null;
                }
                totalAmount = Number(orderQty) * Number(prUnitPrice);
            }
        }

        return totalAmount.toFixed(precision);
    }

    function btnAccountcodeEditClick_AcEmployeeJobDetails(e) {
        e.preventDefault();

        var key = 'AcEmployeeJobDetails';
        var dv = 'MultipleAccountCodeDataView';
        var stgIdFN = 'AccountStagingId';
        var unitsFN = '';
        var unitPriceFN = '';
        var amountFN = 'TotalAmnt';
        var errFN = 'EmployeeJobDetail_Error';
        var msg = 'Salary is required before account allocation.';
        var precision = 2;

        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", errFN);

        var accountCode = $('#tbAccountCodeEdit_' + key + 'acTextBox').val();
        var stagingId = $("#" + stgIdFN).val();
        var totalAmount = AcMultipleAllocation_GetTotalAmount(unitsFN, unitPriceFN, amountFN, true, precision);
        if (totalAmount == null || totalAmount == 'undefined') {
            ShowAjaxMessage(msg, "error", errFN);
            return;
        }

        var data = {
            accountCode: accountCode,
            stagingId: stagingId,
            Amount: totalAmount,
            dataview: dv,
            adjustAllocation: true,
                distributeStagingAmount: true,
            saveAllocationToUserSettings: true,
            acMultipleAccountCodeGrid: true,
            cycleId: '0'
        };
        var dataGrid = {
            DataView: 'MultipleAccountCodeDataView',
            AccountStagingId: '0',
            Key: 'AcEmployeeJobDetails',
            AmountFieldName: 'TotalAmnt',
            TotalHoursFieldName: '',
            HourlyRateFieldName: '',
            AccountStagingIdFieldName: 'AccountStagingId',
            AccountType: 'Expenditure',
            IsViewOnly: 'False',
            CycleId: '0'
        };

        var height = ('False' === 'False' ? 500 : 420);
        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/ProcessAccountCodeAllocation",
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success == true) {
                    var modelKey = 'AcEmployeeJobDetails';
                    var accStagingId = (dataGrid.AccountStagingId == 0 ? (jQuery.isNumeric(result.StagingId) ? result.StagingId : 0) : dataGrid.AccountStagingId).toString();
                    dataGrid.AccountStagingId = accStagingId;
                    var w = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_" + modelKey)
                        .SetContent({
                            type: "POST",
                            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/AcMultipleAccountCodeGrid",
                            data: dataGrid
                        })
                        .SetIsModal(true)
                        .SetWidth(960)
                        .SetHeight(height)
                        .IsRetainHeight(false)
                        .SetTitle("Account Code Allocation")
                        .SetonActivate(function () { eval("onActivateAccountsPopup_" + modelKey + "()"); })
                        .SetonClose(function (e) { if (w.GetDialogResult() != 'Cancel') eval("onCloseRefreshAccountCode_" + modelKey + "()"); });

                    $("#" + stgIdFN).val(result.StagingId);
                    $("#hdnAccountStagingIdEdit_" + key).val(result.StagingId);
                    $("#hdnAccountStagingId_MultipleAccountCodeGrid_" + key).val(result.StagingId);
                    $('#tbAccountCodeGrid_' + key).val('');
                    $("#tbAmountGrid_" + key).val('');

                    RemoveTabRestrictiononPopup();
                    setFocusEventForKendoWindow('popupMultipleAccountCodeGrid_' + key);
                    w.CreateWindow(true);
                    RegisterScreenShortCutKeys(null, key, key);
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error", errFN);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    $(function () {
        $("#btnAccountcodeEdit_AcEmployeeJobDetails").click(btnAccountcodeEditClick_AcEmployeeJobDetails);
    });

    function showErrorMessageForAccountCodeEdit(message) {
        if ($("#" + 'EmployeeJobDetail_Error') != null &amp;&amp; $("#" + 'EmployeeJobDetail_Error') != '') {
            $("#" + 'EmployeeJobDetail_Error').html(message);
            $("#" + 'EmployeeJobDetail_Error').addClass("global_message error");
        }
        else {
            ShowAjaxMessage(message, "error");
        }
    }

<script>

    var smallImageSource = '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/Employee/Photo?id=-1';
    $('#btnCancel__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function (e) {
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
        UnRegisterActiveScreen()
    })

    $('#btnSave__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        EmployeeJobSave(false,false,e);
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").SetTitle('Edit Employee Job');
    });

    $('#btnSaveAndNext__'+'EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        EmployeeJobSave(true,false,e);
    });

    $('#btnSaveAndAdd__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function (e) {
        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").SetTitle('Add Employee Job')
        e.preventDefault();
        EmployeeJobSave(false,true,e);
    });

    $('#btnApprove__EmployeeJobsDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "", "EmployeeJobDetail_Error");

        ShowYesNoDialog('Approve Job', "Are you sure you want to approve the selected job(s)?"
            , function() {$.when(EmployeeJobSave(false,false,e))
                            .then(function () { ApproveJobDate(e); });})
    });

    var eventArgs;

    $('#btnSubmitJobToPayroll__'+'EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        eventArgs = e;
        ShowYesNoDialog("Confirm", "Are you sure you want to submit selected job(s) to payroll?", function () {
            ShowPayrollTransactionDateDialog("False", "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployee/ShowTransactionEncumbranceDialog",
                SubmitJobToPayrollFunction, "SubmitJobToPayrollFunction", null , "-1~5~0", "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollEmployee/IsAtleastOneJobWithEncumbranceExists"
                    , "Submit Job To Payroll", "Job", "")
        });
    });

    $('#btnRemoveJobFromPayroll__'+'EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {

    function RemoveJobFromPayrollFunction(transactionDate){

    function SubmitJobToPayrollFunction(transactionDate){
        SubmitJobToPayroll(-1,5,0, transactionDate);
    }

    function SubmitJobToPayroll(EmployeeId,CycleId,JobSequence,transactionDate) {
        var data;
        data = { EmployeeId: EmployeeId, CycleId: CycleId, JobSequence: JobSequence, transactionDate: transactionDate };

        $.ajax({
            cache: false,
            url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/SubmitJobToPayroll",
            data: data,
            type: "POST",
            success: function (result) {
                if (result != null &amp;&amp; result.Success) {

                    var navigationID = 0;
                    if(EmployeeJobDataView != null &amp;&amp; EmployeeJobDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; EmployeeJobDataView != '' )
                    {
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }
                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__'+'EmployeeJobDataView').is(":visible")){
                        navigationID = '';
                    }
                    else {
                        navigationID = '';
                    }
                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(eventArgs.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob",data: {origin:'EMPLOYEE_JOBS' ,id : navigationID ,aptaDataViewSelection:aptaDataViewSelection},type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");

                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                }
            }});
    }

    $('#btnJobClose__'+'EmployeeJobDataView').click(function (e) {

    function CloseJobDate(e)
    {
        var selectedRowIds = '';
        if (typeof selectedRowIds != "undefined" &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds != null &amp;&amp; selectedRowIds.length &gt; 0){

            var encumberWages = ''
            var showTransactionDatesPopup = 'False';

            if (showTransactionDatesPopup === "True" &amp;&amp; encumberWages == "Yes") {
                ShowCloseJobDatePopup("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/JobDetailCloseJobDate?origin=EMPLOYEE_JOBS",e);
            }
            else {
                $("#div"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("AptaDataView").MakeAjaxCall({
                    url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/CloseEmployeeJob',
                    cache: false,
                    data: { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, origin:'EMPLOYEE_JOBS', aptaDataViewSelection: $("#div"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection() },
                    success: function (result) {
                        //refresh grid
                        if (result.Success == true) {
                            var navigationID = 0;
                            if(EmployeeJobDataView != null &amp;&amp; EmployeeJobDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; EmployeeJobDataView != '' )
                            {
                                var grid = $("#"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                                grid.dataSource.read();
                            }
                            if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__'+'EmployeeJobDataView').is(":visible")){
                                navigationID = '';
                            }
                            else {
                                navigationID = '';
                            }
                            var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                            $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob",data: {origin:'EMPLOYEE_JOBS' ,id : navigationID ,aptaDataViewSelection:aptaDataViewSelection},type:"POST"});
                            ShowAjaxMessage("Job closed successfully", "success","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");

                        }
                        else {
                            ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                        }
                    }
                });

            }
        }
    }

    function ResizeImage(imageElement, maxiWidth, maxiHeight) {
        var maxWidth = maxiWidth; // Max width for the image
        var maxHeight = maxiHeight;    // Max height for the image
        var ratio = 0;  // Used for aspect ratio

        var width = $("#EJimageActualWidth").val();
        var height = $("#EJimageActualHeight").val();

        // Check if the current width is larger than the max
        if (width &gt; maxWidth || width &gt; 46) {
            ratio = maxWidth / width;   // get ratio for scaling image
            $("#" + imageElement).css("width", maxWidth); // Set new width
            $("#" + imageElement).css("height", height * ratio);  // Scale height based on ratio
            height = height * ratio;    // Reset height to match scaled image
            width = width * ratio;    // Reset width to match scaled image
        }

        // Check if current height is larger than max
        if (height &gt; maxHeight || height &gt; 46) {
            ratio = maxHeight / height; // get ratio for scaling image
            $("#" + imageElement).css("height", maxHeight);   // Set new height
            $("#" + imageElement).css("width", width * ratio);    // Scale width based on ratio
            width = width * ratio;    // Reset width to match scaled image
        }
    }

    function UpdateImage() {
        $('#EJemployeeSmallImage').hide();

        $('#EJemployeeSmallImage').attr("src", smallImageSource);
        $('#EJemployeeSmallImage').attr("alt", "No Picture");

        $("#EJimageActualWidth").val('46');
        $("#EJimageActualHeight").val('46');
        ResizeImage("EJemployeeSmallImage", 46, 46);

        $('#EJemployeeSmallImage').show();

        $(".EJEmployeeImageSection").mouseenter(function () {
            $('#EJemployeeSmallImage').css("position", "absolute");
            ResizeImage("EJemployeeSmallImage", 250, 250);
            $('#EJfirstTD').css({ "margin-left": "46px" });
        });

        $(".EJEmployeeImageSection").mouseleave(function () {
            $('#EJemployeeSmallImage').css("position", "relative");
            ResizeImage("EJemployeeSmallImage", 46, 46);
        });
    }

    function ShowCloseJobDatePopup(contentURL,e) {

                                                    var grid = $("#"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                                                    grid.dataSource.read();

                                                if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__'+'EmployeeJobDataView').is(":visible")){
                                                    $("#EmployeeJobsDetailCloseJobDatePopup").data("kendoWindow").close();
                                                    navigationID = '';
                                                }
                                                else {
                                                    navigationID = '';
                                                }
                                                var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                                                $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob",data: {origin:'EMPLOYEE_JOBS', id : navigationID ,aptaDataViewSelection:aptaDataViewSelection},type:"POST"});
                                                ShowAjaxMessage("Job closed successfully", "success","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                                            }
                                        })
    .SetWidth('500')
    .SetHeight('170')
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    }

    function ApproveJobs(e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
        var selectedRowIds = '';

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/ApproveSingleJobFromDetail',
            cache: false,
            data: { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds },
            success: function (result) {

                //refresh grid
                if (result.Success == true) {
                    var navigationID = 0;
                    if(EmployeeJobDataView != null &amp;&amp; EmployeeJobDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; EmployeeJobDataView != '' )
                    {
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }
                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__'+'EmployeeJobDataView').is(":visible")){
                        navigationID = '';
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                    }
                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob",data: {origin:'EMPLOYEE_JOBS' ,id : navigationID ,aptaDataViewSelection:aptaDataViewSelection},type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Job approved successfully.", "success","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");

                }
                else {

                    if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.Message.indexOf('This job is part of a Payroll Register that is currently being processed') != "-1") {
                        ShowYesNoDialog("Approve Job", result.Message, function () { ApproveJobsWithWarning('false', e); });
                    }
                    else if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.Message.indexOf('exceed the budget') != -1) {
                        ShowYesNoDialog("Approve Job", result.Message, function () { ApproveJobsWithWarning('true', e); });
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                    }
                }

            }
        });
    }

    function ApproveJobsWithWarning(inProcessRegisterWarning, e) {

        var selectedRowIds = '';

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/ApproveSingleJobFromDetail',
            cache: false,
            data: { selectedRecords: selectedRowIds, inProcessRegisterWarning: inProcessRegisterWarning, ApproveJobsWithWarning: true },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == true) {
                    var navigationID = 0;
                    if(EmployeeJobDataView != null &amp;&amp; EmployeeJobDataView != undefined &amp;&amp; EmployeeJobDataView != '' )
                    {
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                    }
                    if(!$('#btnSaveAndNext__'+'EmployeeJobDataView').is(":visible")){
                        navigationID = '';
                    }
                    else{
                        navigationID = '';
                    }
                    var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                    $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob",data: {origin:'EMPLOYEE_JOBS' ,id : navigationID ,aptaDataViewSelection:aptaDataViewSelection},type:"POST"});
                    ShowAjaxMessage("Job approved successfully.", "success","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                }
                else {

                    if (result != "" &amp;&amp; result.Message.indexOf('This job is part of a Payroll Register that is currently being processed') != "-1") {
                        ShowYesNoDialog("Approve Job", result.Message, function () { ApproveJobsWithWarning('false', e); });
                    }
                    else {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                    }

                }

            }
        });
    }

    function ApproveJobDate(e) {
        var encumberWages = ''
        var showTransactionDatesPopup = 'False';

        if (showTransactionDatesPopup === "True" &amp;&amp; encumberWages == "Yes") {
            ShowApproveJobDatePopup("/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/DetailApproveJobDate?origin=EMPLOYEE_JOBS",e);
        }
        else {
            ApproveJobs(e);
        }
    }

    function EmployeeJobSave(saveNext, saveAdd, e) {
        ShowAjaxMessage("", "","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");

        var sendFromApproveClosePO = false;
        if(e &amp;&amp; e.target &amp;&amp; (e.target.id == "btnApprove__EmployeeJobsDataView" || e.target.id == 'btnJobClose__'+'EmployeeJobDataView'))
            sendFromApproveClosePO = true;
        var form = $("#MainJobForm");
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            async: !sendFromApproveClosePO,
            url: form.attr('action'),
            data: form.serialize(),
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
            },
            success: function (result) {
                if (result.Success == true) {
                    if(!sendFromApproveClosePO)
                    {
                        MarkEmployeeRecordAsDirty();

                    }
                    if (saveNext) {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                        var aptaDataViewSelection = $("#div"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("AptaDataView").GetAptaDataViewSelection();
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url : "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob",data: {origin : 'EMPLOYEE_JOBS',id : '',aptaDataViewSelection : aptaDataViewSelection }});
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();

                    }
                    else if (saveAdd) {
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({ url: "/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/CreateJob" + "?employeeID=-1&amp;origin="+'EMPLOYEE_JOBS' });
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        grid.dataSource.read();
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();
                    }
                    else if(0 &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; sendFromApproveClosePO){
                        return true;
                    }
                    else if(0 &gt; 0)
                    {
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow").close();
                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        if(grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined){
                            grid.dataSource.read();}
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success");
                    }
                    else {
                        var Id = result.Id;
                        $(e.target).closest(".k-window-content").data("FINSWindow").UpdateContent({url:"/QAAutom/HumanResources/Admin/Employee/EmployeeJob/EditJob",data:{origin : 'EMPLOYEE_JOBS',id:Id},type:"POST"});

                        var grid = $("#"+'EmployeeJobDataView').data("kendoGrid");
                        if(grid !== null &amp;&amp; grid !== undefined){
                            grid.dataSource.read();}
                        ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "success", "EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                        UnRegisterActiveScreen();

                    }
                }
                else {
                    ShowAjaxMessage(result.Message, "error","EmployeeJobDetail_Error");
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function FixIE10Content() {
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("top", parseFloat(50) + "px");
        $(".FINSWindowbody .content").css("bottom", parseFloat(65) + "px");
    }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var popUp = $(".FINSWindowcontainer").closest(".k-window-content").data("kendoWindow");
        if (popUp !== undefined) {
            var browser = get_browser();
            if (browser.name == 'MSIE' &amp;&amp; (browser.version == 10)) {
                FixIE10Content();
            }
            else {
                $(".FINSWindowbody .content-wrapper").css("position", "relative");
            }
        }

    })
